</span><span class="accordion-item-icon accordion-item-icon-theme-white"><span class="ppcmsnodeweb-1bk0n6-svg-size_md" data-ppui-info="icons_8.24.1__7.46.3" aria-hidden="true" data-ppui="true"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" fill="currentColor" viewBox="0 0 24 24" width="1em" height="1em" data-ppui="true"><path d="M13 5a1 1 0 1 0-2 0v6H5a1 1 0 1 0 0 2h6v6a1 1 0 1 0 2 0v-6h6a1 1 0 1 0 0-2h-6V5z" data-ppui="true"></path></svg></span></span></span></button></h3><div id="accordion-content1" aria-labelledby="accordion-row1" role="region" style="height:0px;opacity:0;display:none"><p class="body-text-style body-text-size-body">Each month, you can go to your PayPal app to select which category gets you 5% cash back.<sup>1</sup> Categories include restaurants, apparel, groceries, fuel, and any others we may add in the future.</p>
</div></div><div class="accordion-item"><h3 class="accordion-item-heading"><button type="button" class="accordion-item-headline" id="accordion-row2" aria-controls="accordion-content2" aria-expanded="false" data-pa-click="{&quot;link&quot;:&quot;accordionItemHeader-Primary-How can I request a physical PayPal Debit Card?&quot;,&quot;event_name&quot;:&quot;consumer_button_cta_clicked&quot;}"><span class="accordion-item-headline-container"><span class="accordion-item-headline-text-container"><span class="accordion-item-headline-text heading-text-style heading-text-size-title">How can I request a physical PayPal Debit Card?</span>
</span><span class="accordion-item-icon accordion-item-icon-theme-white"><span class="ppcmsnodeweb-1bk0n6-svg-size_md" data-ppui-info="icons_8.24.1__7.46.3" aria-hidden="true" data-ppui="true"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" fill="currentColor" viewBox="0 0 24 24" width="1em" height="1em" data-ppui="true"><path d="M13 5a1 1 0 1 0-2 0v6H5a1 1 0 1 0 0 2h6v6a1 1 0 1 0 2 0v-6h6a1 1 0 1 0 0-2h-6V5z" data-ppui="true"></path></svg></span></span></span></button></h3><div id="accordion-content2" aria-labelledby="accordion-row2" role="region" style="height:0px;opacity:0;display:none"><p class="body-text-style body-text-size-body">When you sign up for a PayPal Debit Card, you’ll get a digital card instantly. Use it online. Or add it to your phone’s mobile wallet for easy access.</p>
<p class="body-text-style body-text-size-body">If you’d like a physical card, you’ll need to request it. To request a physical card:</p>
<ol><li class="body-text-style body-text-size-body">Go to your Accounts and choose your PayPal Debit Card</li><li class="body-text-style body-text-size-body">Choose Manage</li><li class="body-text-style body-text-size-body">Choose “Request a physical card”</li></ol>
</div></div><div class="accordion-item"><h3 class="accordion-item-heading"><button type="button" class="accordion-item-headline" id="accordion-row3" aria-controls="accordion-content3" aria-expanded="false" data-pa-click="{&quot;link&quot;:&quot;accordionItemHeader-Primary-How do I activate my physical PayPal Debit Card?&quot;,&quot;event_name&quot;:&quot;consumer_button_cta_clicked&quot;}"><span class="accordion-item-headline-container"><span class="accordion-item-headline-text-container"><span class="accordion-item-headline-text heading-text-style heading-text-size-title">How do I activate my physical PayPal Debit Card?</span>
</span><span class="accordion-item-icon accordion-item-icon-theme-white"><span class="ppcmsnodeweb-1bk0n6-svg-size_md" data-ppui-info="icons_8.24.1__7.46.3" aria-hidden="true" data-ppui="true"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" fill="currentColor" viewBox="0 0 24 24" width="1em" height="1em" data-ppui="true"><path d="M13 5a1 1 0 1 0-2 0v6H5a1 1 0 1 0 0 2h6v6a1 1 0 1 0 2 0v-6h6a1 1 0 1 0 0-2h-6V5z" data-ppui="true"></path></svg></span></span></span></button></h3><div id="accordion-content3" aria-labelledby="accordion-row3" role="region" style="height:0px;opacity:0;display:none"><p class="body-text-style body-text-size-body">Here's how to activate your physical PayPal Debit Card through the PayPal website:</p>
<ol><li class="body-text-style body-text-size-body"><span>Go to </span><a href="https://www.paypal.com/activatecard" target="_self" rel="" class="html-text-renderer-link" data-pa-click="{&quot;link&quot;:&quot;Accordion-Link-Paragraph-paypal.com/activatecard&quot;,&quot;event_name&quot;:&quot;consumer_text_link_clicked&quot;}">paypal.com/activatecard</a></li><li class="body-text-style body-text-size-body">Log in to your account and enter the required information</li><li class="body-text-style body-text-size-body">Choose Activate Card</li></ol>
<p class="body-text-style body-text-size-body">To activate your physical PayPal Debit Card in the app:</p>
<ol><li class="body-text-style body-text-size-body">Go to your Accounts</li><li class="body-text-style body-text-size-body">Choose PayPal Debit Card</li><li class="body-text-style body-text-size-body">Enter the required information</li><li class="body-text-style body-text-size-body">Choose Activate Card</li></ol>
<p class="body-text-style body-text-size-body">You can also activate your physical PayPal Debit Card by calling our 24-hour automated activation line and following the steps provided at 1-800-314-8298.</p>
</div></div><div class="accordion-item"><h3 class="accordion-item-heading"><button type="button" class="accordion-item-headline" id="accordion-row4" aria-controls="accordion-content4" aria-expanded="false" data-pa-click="{&quot;link&quot;:&quot;accordionItemHeader-Primary-Are there any monthly or transaction fees?&quot;,&quot;event_name&quot;:&quot;consumer_button_cta_clicked&quot;}"><span class="accordion-item-headline-container"><span class="accordion-item-headline-text-container"><span class="accordion-item-headline-text heading-text-style heading-text-size-title">Are there any monthly or transaction fees?</span>
</span><span class="accordion-item-icon accordion-item-icon-theme-white"><span class="ppcmsnodeweb-1bk0n6-svg-size_md" data-ppui-info="icons_8.24.1__7.46.3" aria-hidden="true" data-ppui="true"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" fill="currentColor" viewBox="0 0 24 24" width="1em" height="1em" data-ppui="true"><path d="M13 5a1 1 0 1 0-2 0v6H5a1 1 0 1 0 0 2h6v6a1 1 0 1 0 2 0v-6h6a1 1 0 1 0 0-2h-6V5z" data-ppui="true"></path></svg></span></span></span></button></h3><div id="accordion-content4" aria-labelledby="accordion-row4" role="region" style="height:0px;opacity:0;display:none"><p class="body-text-style body-text-size-body"><span>The PayPal Debit Card has no monthly fees and no minimum balance. There's no transaction fee for US purchase transactions. Foreign transactions have a 2.5% international transaction fee. </span><a href="https://www.paypal.com/us/webapps/mpp/paypal-fees" target="_self" rel="" class="html-text-renderer-link" data-pa-click="{&quot;link&quot;:&quot;Accordion-Link-Paragraph-More about pricing&quot;,&quot;event_name&quot;:&quot;consumer_text_link_clicked&quot;}">More about pricing</a><span>.</span></p>
</div></div><div class="accordion-item"><h3 class="accordion-item-heading"><button type="button" class="accordion-item-headline" id="accordion-row5" aria-controls="accordion-content5" aria-expanded="false" data-pa-click="{&quot;link&quot;:&quot;accordionItemHeader-Primary-How do I add money to my PayPal balance?&quot;,&quot;event_name&quot;:&quot;consumer_button_cta_clicked&quot;}"><span class="accordion-item-headline-container"><span class="accordion-item-headline-text-container"><span class="accordion-item-headline-text heading-text-style heading-text-size-title">How do I add money to my PayPal balance?</span>
</span><span class="accordion-item-icon accordion-item-icon-theme-white"><span class="ppcmsnodeweb-1bk0n6-svg-size_md" data-ppui-info="icons_8.24.1__7.46.3" aria-hidden="true" data-ppui="true"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" fill="currentColor" viewBox="0 0 24 24" width="1em" height="1em" data-ppui="true"><path d="M13 5a1 1 0 1 0-2 0v6H5a1 1 0 1 0 0 2h6v6a1 1 0 1 0 2 0v-6h6a1 1 0 1 0 0-2h-6V5z" data-ppui="true"></path></svg></span></span></span></button></h3><div id="accordion-content5" aria-labelledby="accordion-row5" role="region" style="height:0px;opacity:0;display:none"><p class="body-text-style body-text-size-body"><span>Transfer money from a bank account or debit card. Set up auto reload to add money weekly, bi-weekly, monthly, or whenever your balance dips below an amount you choose. You can also have your paychecks sent directly to your PayPal balance with Direct Deposit. </span><a href="https://www.paypal.com/us/digital-wallet/manage-money/add-cash" target="_self" rel="" class="html-text-renderer-link" data-pa-click="{&quot;link&quot;:&quot;Accordion-Link-Paragraph-Check out all the ways to add to your PayPal balance&quot;,&quot;event_name&quot;:&quot;consumer_text_link_clicked&quot;}">Check out all the ways to add to your PayPal balance</a><span>.</span></p>
</div></div><div class="accordion-item"><h3 class="accordion-item-heading"><button type="button" class="accordion-item-headline" id="accordion-row6" aria-controls="accordion-content6" aria-expanded="false" data-pa-click="{&quot;link&quot;:&quot;accordionItemHeader-Primary-How do I check the available balance for my PayPal Debit Card?&quot;,&quot;event_name&quot;:&quot;consumer_button_cta_clicked&quot;}"><span class="accordion-item-headline-container"><span class="accordion-item-headline-text-container"><span class="accordion-item-headline-text heading-text-style heading-text-size-title">How do I check the available balance for my PayPal Debit Card?</span>
</span><span class="accordion-item-icon accordion-item-icon-theme-white"><span class="ppcmsnodeweb-1bk0n6-svg-size_md" data-ppui-info="icons_8.24.1__7.46.3" aria-hidden="true" data-ppui="true"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" fill="currentColor" viewBox="0 0 24 24" width="1em" height="1em" data-ppui="true"><path d="M13 5a1 1 0 1 0-2 0v6H5a1 1 0 1 0 0 2h6v6a1 1 0 1 0 2 0v-6h6a1 1 0 1 0 0-2h-6V5z" data-ppui="true"></path></svg></span></span></span></button></h3><div id="accordion-content6" aria-labelledby="accordion-row6" role="region" style="height:0px;opacity:0;display:none"><p class="body-text-style body-text-size-body">Just open your app and check your PayPal balance. Then pay anywhere Mastercard is accepted.<sup>2</sup></p>
</div></div><div class="accordion-item"><h3 class="accordion-item-heading"><button type="button" class="accordion-item-headline" id="accordion-row7" aria-controls="accordion-content7" aria-expanded="false" data-pa-click="{&quot;link&quot;:&quot;accordionItemHeader-Primary-How do I check my PayPal Rewards points balance?&quot;,&quot;event_name&quot;:&quot;consumer_button_cta_clicked&quot;}"><span class="accordion-item-headline-container"><span class="accordion-item-headline-text-container"><span class="accordion-item-headline-text heading-text-style heading-text-size-title">How do I check my PayPal Rewards points balance?</span>
</span><span class="accordion-item-icon accordion-item-icon-theme-white"><span class="ppcmsnodeweb-1bk0n6-svg-size_md" data-ppui-info="icons_8.24.1__7.46.3" aria-hidden="true" data-ppui="true"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" fill="currentColor" viewBox="0 0 24 24" width="1em" height="1em" data-ppui="true"><path d="M13 5a1 1 0 1 0-2 0v6H5a1 1 0 1 0 0 2h6v6a1 1 0 1 0 2 0v-6h6a1 1 0 1 0 0-2h-6V5z" data-ppui="true"></path></svg></span></span></span></button></h3><div id="accordion-content7" aria-labelledby="accordion-row7" role="region" style="height:0px;opacity:0;display:none"><p class="body-text-style body-text-size-body">You can track your PayPal Rewards points and redeem them for cash back in the Rewards hub. Just click the trophy icon in the PayPal app.</p>
</div></div><div class="accordion-item"><h3 class="accordion-item-heading"><button type="button" class="accordion-item-headline" id="accordion-row8" aria-controls="accordion-content8" aria-expanded="false" data-pa-click="{&quot;link&quot;:&quot;accordionItemHeader-Primary-Can I add my PayPal Debit Card to a mobile wallet?&quot;,&quot;event_name&quot;:&quot;consumer_button_cta_clicked&quot;}"><span class="accordion-item-headline-container"><span class="accordion-item-headline-text-container"><span class="accordion-item-headline-text heading-text-style heading-text-size-title">Can I add my PayPal Debit Card to a mobile wallet?</span>
</span><span class="accordion-item-icon accordion-item-icon-theme-white"><span class="ppcmsnodeweb-1bk0n6-svg-size_md" data-ppui-info="icons_8.24.1__7.46.3" aria-hidden="true" data-ppui="true"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" fill="currentColor" viewBox="0 0 24 24" width="1em" height="1em" data-ppui="true"><path d="M13 5a1 1 0 1 0-2 0v6H5a1 1 0 1 0 0 2h6v6a1 1 0 1 0 2 0v-6h6a1 1 0 1 0 0-2h-6V5z" data-ppui="true"></path></svg></span></span></span></button></h3><div id="accordion-content8" aria-labelledby="accordion-row8" role="region" style="height:0px;opacity:0;display:none"><p class="body-text-style body-text-size-body"><span>Yes, you can add your PayPal Debit Card to your smartphone’s mobile wallet. Then you can make contactless payments using Apple Pay®, Google Pay, and Samsung Pay. </span><a href="https://www.paypal.com/us/campaign/mobile-wallets" target="_self" rel="" class="html-text-renderer-link" data-pa-click="{&quot;link&quot;:&quot;Accordion-Link-Paragraph-Learn how to add your card to your mobile wallet&quot;,&quot;event_name&quot;:&quot;consumer_text_link_clicked&quot;}">Learn how to add your card to your mobile wallet</a><span>.</span></p>
</div></div><div class="accordion-item"><h3 class="accordion-item-heading"><button type="button" class="accordion-item-headline" id="accordion-row9" aria-controls="accordion-content9" aria-expanded="false" data-pa-click="{&quot;link&quot;:&quot;accordionItemHeader-Primary-Can I use my PayPal Debit Card at an ATM? Are there fees?&quot;,&quot;event_name&quot;:&quot;consumer_button_cta_clicked&quot;}"><span class="accordion-item-headline-container"><span class="accordion-item-headline-text-container"><span class="accordion-item-headline-text heading-text-style heading-text-size-title">Can I use my PayPal Debit Card at an ATM? Are there fees?</span>
</span><span class="accordion-item-icon accordion-item-icon-theme-white"><span class="ppcmsnodeweb-1bk0n6-svg-size_md" data-ppui-info="icons_8.24.1__7.46.3" aria-hidden="true" data-ppui="true"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" fill="currentColor" viewBox="0 0 24 24" width="1em" height="1em" data-ppui="true"><path d="M13 5a1 1 0 1 0-2 0v6H5a1 1 0 1 0 0 2h6v6a1 1 0 1 0 2 0v-6h6a1 1 0 1 0 0-2h-6V5z" data-ppui="true"></path></svg></span></span></span></button></h3><div id="accordion-content9" aria-labelledby="accordion-row9" role="region" style="height:0px;opacity:0;display:none"><p class="body-text-style body-text-size-body">To withdraw funds from your PayPal balance, simply use the card and the PIN you created when you activated the card. There's no fee for withdrawing cash from MoneyPass ATMs across the U.S.<sup>4</sup> Withdrawals from non-MoneyPass ATMs have a $2.50 ATM withdrawal fee.</p>
</div></div></div></section><!--/$--><!--$--><section class="text-section section-wrapper blue-600-plate grid ppe ppe-palette grid-compact ppcmsnodeweb-d0h82c" style="opacity:0;transform:translateX(0rem) translateY(0rem) scale(1) translateZ(0)"><div class="text-header-inner text-section-alignment-12-col-start-to-end ppcmsnodeweb-1trm3rd"><div class="text-group text-group-alignment-start" style="opacity:0;transform:translateX(0.75px) translateY(0.75px) scale(1) translateZ(0)"><div style="opacity:0;transform:translateX(0.75rem) translateY(0.75rem) scale(1) translateZ(0)"><h2 class="text-group-headline heading-text-style heading-text-size-headline-4">Find more ways to manage your money</h2>

IMPORTANT INFORMATION ABOUT PROCEDURES FOR OPENING A NEW CARD ACCOUNT: To help the government fight the funding of
terrorism and money laundering activities, federal law requires all financial institutions to obtain, verify, and record information that identifies each person who opens a Card Account. What this means for you: When you open a Card Account, we will ask for your name, address, date of birth, and other information that will allow us to identify you. Funds deposited via Direct Deposit will generally be available on the day we receive the funds transfer. You may review activity on your periodic statements or transaction history on www.PayPal.com, or call Customer Service at 1-888-221-1161 to verify receipt. We reserve the right to accept, reject, or limit transfers via Direct Deposit in our sole discretion. If you wish to cancel Direct Deposits, you must contact your employer. PayPal does not charge any fee to set up or maintain Direct Deposit. Refer to your </span><a href="https://www.paypal.com/us/legalhub/pp-balance-tnc" target="_self" rel="" class="html-text-renderer-link multi-line-text-paragraph" data-pa-click="{&quot;link&quot;:&quot;Disclosure-Link--PayPal Balance Terms and Conditions&quot;,&quot;event_name&quot;:&quot;consumer_text_link_clicked&quot;}">PayPal Balance Terms and Conditions</a><span> for complete Direct Deposit details. Once it's set up, Direct Deposit usually takes two (2) pay cycles to begin, but can vary across employers. Please check with your employer for specific timing.</span></div>
</div><div class="disclosure-item multi-line-text body-text-style body-text-size-caption"><div class="multi-line-text-sup"><sup>9</sup></div><div class="multi-line-text-paragraph">Early access can allow a user to access their funds up to 2 days early. Early access to funds depends on when we get payment instructions from the payor (your employer or government agency). When we get funds before the scheduled payment date, your money can be made available up to 2 days sooner than scheduled. Availability and timing can vary based on the payor and when we get payment instructions. Once the funds are received, they will be deposited directly into your PayPal balance.</div>

</div><div class="disclosure-item multi-line-text multi-line-text-wo-sup body-text-style body-text-size-caption"><div class="multi-line-text-paragraph">Effective February 14, 2022, Cash a Check is no longer available to PayPal customers located in New York.</div>
</div><div class="disclosure-item multi-line-text body-text-style body-text-size-caption"><div class="multi-line-text-sup"><sup>12</sup></div><div class="multi-line-text-paragraph">Up to $3.95 cash reload fee applies. This service fee is to add cash into your PayPal Balance account.</div>
</div><div class="disclosure-item multi-line-text body-text-style body-text-size-caption"><div class="multi-line-text-sup"><sup>13</sup></div><div class="multi-line-text-paragraph"><span>PayPal Purchase Protection is available on eligible transactions. </span><a href="https://www.paypal.com/us/legalhub/buyer-protection" target="_self" rel="" class="html-text-renderer-link multi-line-text-paragraph" data-pa-click="{&quot;link&quot;:&quot;Disclosure-Link--Terms and limitations apply&quot;,&quot;event_name&quot;:&quot;consumer_text_link_clicked&quot;}">Terms and limitations apply</a><span>.</span></div>
</div><div class="disclosure-item multi-line-text body-text-style body-text-size-caption"><div class="multi-line-text-sup"><sup>14</sup></div><div class="multi-line-text-paragraph"><span>Conditions and exceptions apply – see </span><a href="https://www.paypal.com/us/legalhub/consumer-debitcard-agreement?locale.x=en_US" target="_self" rel="" class="html-text-renderer-link multi-line-text-paragraph" data-pa-click="{&quot;link&quot;:&quot;Disclosure-Link--Cardholder Agreement&quot;,&quot;event_name&quot;:&quot;consumer_text_link_clicked&quot;}">Cardholder Agreement</a><span>.</span></div>
